      <title>Never Say Never: How Parenting Humbled Us</title>
      <itunes:title>Never Say Never: How Parenting Humbled Us</itunes:title>
      <description><![CDATA[<p>Remember all those things you swore you&rsquo;d never do when you had kids? Well, we're taking a trip down memory lane and laughing about all our parenting promises that went out the window. From screen time rules to picky eating battles, we cover it all. Plus, we share some absolute crackers from our Sh*tters.       <title>Dear Millennials: Remember How Embarrassing The 90s Were?</title>
      <itunes:title>Dear Millennials: Remember How Embarrassing The 90s Were?</itunes:title>
      <description><![CDATA[<p>Millennials, gather round. This week on <em>Eat Sleep Repeat</em>, Kelly and Lize realise the kids have officially left us behind. When exactly did we become the adults who &ldquo;just don&rsquo;t get it&rdquo;? And more importantly - did we forget just how cringe <em>we</em> were?</p> <p>From &ldquo;talk to the hand,&rdquo; fo&rsquo; shizzle, and calling absolutely everything gay (yikes), to marbles, mix CDs, MSN acronyms and pranks that would 100% get you suspended today - the girls take a nostalgic, humiliating walk through millennial childhood. A gentle reminder that maybe neither generation has the moral high ground here.</p> <p><strong><br>LINKS TO EVERYTHING MENTIONED<br></strong><a href="https://www.thecut.com/article/what-does-six-seven-slang-mean.html">The 67 Trend - The Cut</a> <br><a href="https://www.netflix.com/au/title/82018736">The Perfect Neighbor - Netflix</a><br><a href="https://amzn.to/4hzfpnu">Darning Kit <br></a><a href="https://wearnala.com/?srsltid=AfmBOoozIDwZzeQ7kKufHrLUKh-lKkb_VVdX81FujZpoqOoElR47sE6G">Wear Nala</a></p> <p><strong>&nbsp;<br>HOSTS &amp; PRODUCERS<br></strong>Kelly McCarren&nbsp;⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠<a href="https://www.instagram.com/kelly_mccarren/">⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠@kelly_mccarren⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠</a><br>Lize Ratliff - <a href="https://www.instagram.com/lizaratliff/?hl=en">@lizaratliff</a><br><br><strong>AUDIO PRODUCTION<br></strong>Madeline Joannou - <a href="www.mylkmedia.com.au">⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠Mylk Media⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠</a>&nbsp;⁠⁠⁠⁠</p><p>See <a href="https://omnystudio.com/listener">omnystudio.com/listener</a> for privacy information.</p>]]></description>

      <title>The Dark Side of Postpartum: My Time in a Psych Ward</title>
      <itunes:title>The Dark Side of Postpartum: My Time in a Psych Ward</itunes:title>
      <description><![CDATA[<p>Content Warning: This episode discusses themes that may be upsetting. We discuss postpartum depression and psychosis, suicidal ideation, overdose, severe mental health issues and disassociation. Listener discretion is advised.</p> <p>The postpartum period can be one of the most isolating and lonely times of someone's life. You've just grown and birthed an entire human, your hormones are all over the shop, and you're keeping your little one alive while sleep-deprived and trying to remember the person you once were. It's often not a great recipe, yet we're still sold the idea of bliss being wrapped up in a 'newborn bubble'.</p> <p>In this episode, Kel and Kee discuss their own experiences with postpartum mental health and chat with someone whose experience led her to a psychiatric facility only weeks post-birth. This is an honest and raw conversation; let it remind you that you're never alone.</p> <p>If you or someone you know is in crisis and needs help now, call triple zero (000). You can also call Lifeline on 13 11 14 -&nbsp; 24 hours a day, 7 days a week.</p> <p>PANDA (Perinatal Anxiety &amp; Depression Australia) supports women, men and families across Australia affected by anxiety and depression during pregnancy and in the first year of parenthood. Call 1300 726 306, 9am &ndash; 7:30pm AEST (Mon-Fri).</p> <p><strong>&nbsp;<br>HOSTS &amp; PRODUCERS<br></strong>Kelly McCarren&nbsp;⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠<a href="https://www.instagram.com/kelly_mccarren/">⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠@kelly_mccarren⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠</a><br>Kee Reece Searles <a href="https://www.instagram.com/keereece/?hl=en">@keereece</a></p> <p><br><strong>AUDIO PRODUCTION<br></strong>Madeline Joannou - <a href="www.mylkmedia.com.au">⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠Mylk Media⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠</a> ⁠⁠⁠⁠</p><p>See <a href="https://omnystudio.com/listener">omnystudio.com/listener</a> for privacy information.</p>]]></description>
      <content:encoded><![CDATA[<p>Content Warning: This episode discusses themes that may be upsetting. We discuss postpartum depression and psychosis, suicidal ideation, overdose, severe mental health issues and disassociation. Listener discretion is advised.</p> <p>The postpartum period can be one of the most isolating and lonely times of someone's life. You've just grown and birthed an entire human, your hormones are all over the shop, and you're keeping your little one alive while sleep-deprived and trying to remember the person you once were. It's often not a great recipe, yet we're still sold the idea of bliss being wrapped up in a 'newborn bubble'.</p> <p>In this episode, Kel and Kee discuss their own experiences with postpartum mental health and chat with someone whose experience led her to a psychiatric facility only weeks post-birth. This is an honest and raw conversation; let it remind you that you're never alone.</p> <p>If you or someone you know is in crisis and needs help now, call triple zero (000). You can also call Lifeline on 13 11 14 -&nbsp; 24 hours a day, 7 days a week.</p> <p>PANDA (Perinatal Anxiety &amp; Depression Australia) supports women, men and families across Australia affected by anxiety and depression during pregnancy and in the first year of parenthood. Call 1300 726 306, 9am &ndash; 7:30pm AEST (Mon-Fri).</p> <p><strong>&nbsp;<br>HOSTS &amp; PRODUCERS<br></strong>Kelly McCarren&nbsp;⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠<a href="https://www.instagram.com/kelly_mccarren/">⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠@kelly_mccarren⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠</a><br>Kee Reece Searles <a href="https://www.instagram.com/keereece/?hl=en">@keereece</a></p> <p><br><strong>AUDIO PRODUCTION<br></strong>Madeline Joannou - <a href="www.mylkmedia.com.au">⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠Mylk Media⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠</a> ⁠⁠⁠⁠</p><p>See <a href="https://omnystudio.com/listener">omnystudio.com/listener</a> for privacy information.</p>]]></content:encoded>

      <title>I Had A Baby And Quit My Dream Job</title>

      <description><![CDATA[<p>What happens when you finally land your dream job&hellip;and then realise it no longer fits the life you want? Lize Ratliff spent a decade at Mamamia and rose to Head of Podcasts, but when motherhood arrived she felt the pull of something different. In this candid chat with Kelly and Kee, Lize shares why she left Sydney, swapped a high-pressure career for Newcastle&rsquo;s slower pace, and went back to uni to become a teacher.</p> <p>It&rsquo;s a refreshingly honest conversation about identity, ambition, and choosing family and freedom over titles - and why that might be the boldest career move of all.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><strong>LINKS TO EVERYTHING MENTIONED<br></strong><a href="https://www.darlingharbour.com/stay/hyatt-regency-sydney">Hyatt Regency Staycation</a><br><a href="https://www.spoilmekidsdayspa.com.au/">Spoil Me Kids Day Spa</a><br><a href="https://mothercraftforbabies.com.au/">Mothercraft for Babies</a><br><a href="https://www.instagram.com/mothercraft4babies_?igsh=YWNtOWlybHVzZXB21941.html">Mothercraft for Babies Instagram</a></p> <p><strong><br>HOSTS &amp; PRODUCERS<br></strong>Kelly McCarren&nbsp;⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠<a href="https://www.instagram.com/kelly_mccarren/">⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠@kelly_mccarren⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠</a><br>Kee Reece Searles <a href="https://www.instagram.com/keereece/?hl=en">⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠@keereece⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠</a><br><br><strong>AUDIO PRODUCTION<br></strong>Madeline Joannou - <a href="www.mylkmedia.com.au">⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠Mylk Media⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠</a>&nbsp;⁠⁠⁠⁠</p><p>See <a href="https://omnystudio.com/listener">omnystudio.com/listener</a> for privacy information.</p>]]></description>

      <title>I Don’t Want To Parent The Way I Was Parented</title>
      <itunes:title>I Don’t Want To Parent The Way I Was Parented</itunes:title>
      <description><![CDATA[<p>Ever caught yourself mid-meltdown and thought, &ldquo;Oh no&hellip; I&rsquo;ve turned into my mum&rdquo;? In this episode, Kee opens up about the confronting realisation that breaking toxic family patterns is so much harder than it sounds - especially when you're sleep-deprived, overstimulated, and raising a tiny dictator. She and Kelly unpack the parenting styles they grew up with, how those experiences shaped them, and the values they&rsquo;re trying to pass on to their own kids. There&rsquo;s a powerful three-question exercise in here that&rsquo;ll make you think differently about your own upbringing, and remind you that even when it feels like you&rsquo;re getting it wrong, the fact that you care means you&rsquo;re already doing better than you think.</p> <p><br><strong>LINKS TO EVERYTHING MENTIONED</strong></p> <p><a href="https://www.playgroundequipment.com/23-parenting-philosophies-and-methods-explained/">Parenting Philosophies</a></p> <p><a href="https://brenebrown.com/resources/dare-to-lead-list-of-values/">Bren&eacute; Brown's List of Values</a></p> <p>Article - <a href="https://www.parents.com/what-does-it-mean-to-break-the-cycle-if-your-family-is-toxic-11737794">Breaking the Cycle of Toxic Family Behavior Is Hard</a></p> <p><a href="https://www.deanatynan.com.au/shop">"Pepe and the Secret Sauce" by Deana Tynan</a></p> <p><a href="https://www.naturebaby.com.au/shop?q=lambskin+booties">Nature Baby Lambskin Booties</a></p> <p><a href="https://www.harpercollins.com.au/9780008601584/its-always-the-husband/">"It's Always The Husband" by C.L.       <title>Please Stop Telling Me My Son’s Autistic</title>
      <itunes:title>Please Stop Telling Me My Son’s Autistic</itunes:title>
      <description><![CDATA[<p>There’s nothing quite like the internet to make you feel like a sh*t parent when you’re just trying to raise a toddler and post the occasional cute video. And look, we get it - people mean well. But when Kel shares a moment from life with her three year old and ends up fielding DMs diagnosing him with autism, it starts to feel less like support and more like unsolicited parenting advice from strangers on the internet. In this episode, we’re talking boundaries, overdiagnosis, and the emotional whiplash of parenting publicly in the age of constant commentary.</p><p><br><strong>LINKS TO EVERYTHING MENTIONED</strong></p><p><a href="https://www.instagram.com/p/DK6pGGwTzFH/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferer">Baby Food Bible Healthy Muffin Recipe</a></p><p><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/list/185286612-kelly-mccarren?order=d&shelf=short-stories&sort=date_added" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferer">The Goodread&#39;s Staff Summer Picks</a></p><p><br></p><p><strong>HOSTS &amp; PRODUCERS</strong></p><p>Kelly McCarren ⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠<a href="https://www.instagram.com/kelly_mccarren/">⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠@kelly_mccarren⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠</a></p><p>Kee Reece Searles <a href="https://www.instagram.com/keereece/?hl=en">⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠@keereece⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠</a></p><p><br></p><p><strong>AUDIO PRODUCTION</strong></p><p>Madeline Joannou - <a href="www.mylkmedia.com.au">⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠Mylk Media⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠</a> ⁠⁠⁠⁠</p><p>See <a href="https://omnystudio.com/listener">omnystudio.com/listener</a> for privacy information.</p>]]></description>
      <content:encoded><![CDATA[<p>There’s nothing quite like the internet to make you feel like a sh*t parent when you’re just trying to raise a toddler and post the occasional cute video. And look, we get it - people mean well. But when Kel shares a moment from life with her three year old and ends up fielding DMs diagnosing him with autism, it starts to feel less like support and more like unsolicited parenting advice from strangers on the internet. In this episode, we’re talking boundaries, overdiagnosis, and the emotional whiplash of parenting publicly in the age of constant commentary.</p><p><br><strong>LINKS TO EVERYTHING MENTIONED</strong></p><p><a href="https://www.instagram.com/p/DK6pGGwTzFH/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferer">Baby Food Bible Healthy Muffin Recipe</a></p><p><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/list/185286612-kelly-mccarren?order=d&shelf=short-stories&sort=date_added" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferer">The Goodread&#39;s Staff Summer Picks</a></p><p><br></p><p><strong>HOSTS &amp; PRODUCERS</strong></p><p>Kelly McCarren ⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠<a href="https://www.instagram.com/kelly_mccarren/">⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠@kelly_mccarren⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠</a></p><p>Kee Reece Searles <a href="https://www.instagram.com/keereece/?hl=en">⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠@keereece⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠</a></p><p><br></p><p><strong>AUDIO PRODUCTION</strong></p><p>Madeline Joannou - <a href="www.mylkmedia.com.au">⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠Mylk Media⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠</a> ⁠⁠⁠⁠</p><p>See <a href="https://omnystudio.com/listener">omnystudio.com/listener</a> for privacy information.</p>]]></content:encoded>

      <title>You're Not 'Just' A Mum</title>
      <itunes:title>You're Not 'Just' A Mum</itunes:title>
      <description><![CDATA[<p>Apparently once you have a baby, your only acceptable form of fun is a pedicure and an occasional massage - and we call bullshit.</p><p>This week, Kel gets fired up about the idea that mothers have to <em>earn</em> their joy, especially when that joy looks like getting a little loose.       <title>My Son and I Shared a Womb</title>
      <itunes:title>My Son and I Shared a Womb</itunes:title>
      <description><![CDATA[<p>This is the kind of story that stops you in your tracks. When Kristy Bryant lost her uterus after a traumatic birth, she thought her dream of carrying another child was over. But in an extraordinary Australia-first clinical trial, she received a uterus transplant - from her own mother, Michelle. That same womb, which once carried Kristy, gave her the chance to carry her son, Henry.</p><p><br></p><p>Kristy takes us inside this groundbreaking procedure, sparing no details. With raw honesty, she shares the highs, the heartbreak, and the deeply personal (and at times graphic) realities of this medical milestone, all made possible by the ultimate mother-daughter bond.</p><p><br></p><p><strong>HOSTS &amp; PRODUCERS</strong></p><p>Kelly McCarren ⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠<a href="https://www.instagram.com/kelly_mccarren/">⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠@kelly_mccarren⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠</a></p><p>Kee Reece<a href="https://www.instagram.com/keereece/">⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠@keereece⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠</a></p><p><br></p><p><strong>AUDIO PRODUCTION</strong></p><p>Madeline Joannou -<a href="www.mylkmedia.com.au">⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠Mylk Media⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠</a> ⁠⁠⁠⁠</p><p>See <a href="https://omnystudio.com/listener">omnystudio.com/listener</a> for privacy information.</p>]]></description>

      <title>The Lonely Parents Club And How To Make Friends</title>
      <itunes:title>The Lonely Parents Club And How To Make Friends</itunes:title>
      <description><![CDATA[<p>Parenting can be lonely - but it doesn’t have to be! In this episode of <em>Eat Sleep Sh*t Repeat</em>, Kee and Kelly share their wild and wonderful stories about making friends as parents. They reveal surprising and sometimes hilarious ways they've built their support networks.<br>If you’re feeling isolated or just need some fresh ideas on how to meet your “parent people,” this one’s for you.       <description><![CDATA[<p>Are you stuck with most of the parenting duties? Wondering how to get your partner to share the load? In this episode of <em>Eat Sleep Sh*t Repeat</em>, Kelly and Kee dive into the often-overlooked mental and physical burdens many parents face, and how to actually make a change.       <content:encoded><![CDATA[<p>Talking to kids about disability can feel tricky, but it's a conversation that helps build empathy, understanding, and inclusivity from a young age. This week, Kee and Kelly are joined by Peta Hooke, host of 'The I Can’t Stand Podcast' and self-described as "your friendly girl next door who has a disability."       <description><![CDATA[<p>Diet culture sneaks into so many aspects of our lives, and it can be hard to spot just how toxic it is - especially when it’s been normalised for so long. In this episode, Kee and Kelly dive into their personal experiences with body image and diet culture, unpacking how it affected them and what they've learned along the way.       <title>Mummy Wine Culture Isn't Cute</title>

      <title>Traveling Europe With A Toddler Will Be Fun (Said No One)</title>
      <itunes:title>Traveling Europe With A Toddler Will Be Fun (Said No One)</itunes:title>

      <title>Why All New Mothers Need Mothering</title>

      <description><![CDATA[<p>The 4th trimester isn’t always the blissful baby bubble people make it out to be. For many new mothers, it’s a time of fear, loneliness, and isolation—especially in a culture where the village is nowhere to be found. </p> <p>In this episode, we’re joined by Larissa Leone, Founder of Homb, to talk about the crucial need for post-birth aftercare and why all new mothers need mothering, too. We’ll dive into what that support should look like in an ideal world and how we can better care for mothers during this vulnerable time.</p> <p><strong>RESOURCES</strong></p> <p><a href="https://shebirths.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferer">She Births</a></p> <p><a href="https://homb.com.au/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferer">Homb Postpartum Support</a></p> <p><a href="https://panda.org.au/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferer">PANDA National Helpline</a> - 1300 726 306</p> <p><a href="https://www.parentline.org.au/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferer">Parentline</a></p> <p><a href="https://www.gidgetfoundation.org.au/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferer">Gidget Foundation Australia</a></p> <p><a href="https://www.mumformum.org.au/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferer">Mum for Mum </a></p> <p><a href="https://peachtree.org.au/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferer">Peach Tree</a> - Perinatal Wellness</p> <p><a href="https://www.sydneyconcierge.com.au/product/new-mum-packages/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferer">Sydney Concierge New Mum Packages</a></p> <p><a href="https://www.playgroupaustralia.o" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferer">Playgroup Australia</a></p> <p><a href="https://www.mamatribe.com.au/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferer">Mama Tribe</a> - Meet Local Mamas</p> <p><a href="https://www.mumspace.com.au/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferer">Mum Space</a> - Mental Health Support for Mums</p> <p><a href="https://raisingchildren.net.au/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferer">The Australian Parenting Website</a></p> <p><a href="https://www.tresillian.org.au/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferer">Tresillian</a></p> <p><a href="https://karitane.com.au/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferer">Karitane</a></p> <p><a href="https://www.cope.org.au/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferer">COPE Centre of Perinatal Excellence</a></p> <p><strong>HOSTS &amp;       <description><![CDATA[<p>Raising biracial kids in a whitewashed world comes with its own unique set of challenges and joys. </p> <p>In this episode, we delve into the intricacies of ensuring your children stay connected to their diverse cultural heritage.       <title>Back To Work, Now What?</title>
      <itunes:title>Back To Work, Now What?</itunes:title>
      <description><![CDATA[<p>Last season we unpacked the process of sending your kid to daycare &amp; all the fun that comes with it (the bugs, mainly the bugs) so today we&#39;re discussing the logistics of going back to work.</p> <p>You already know our personal back to work stories, Kee went back after a year &amp; then threw in the towel to freelance and Kel just took no time off at all. So today we&#39;re chatting to two glorious Sh*tters (Sandy &amp; Lily) who have had very different experiences entering back into the workforce.</p> <p>Sandy is a mum to 3 young kids, who not only juggles her own nursing career, but also supports her husband who&#39;s currently studying to become a surgeon.</p> <p>Lily is a mum of one, with another on the way, whose identity completely changed after becoming a first time mum. This led to a return-to-work at four months postpartum, a career change and another (career) baby; Launch Mama, a program dedicated to helping mums navigate their transition back into the workforce.</p> <p>MENTIONS</p> <p>2024 Kokoda Ladies Trek - <a href="https://mhfkokodatrek.gofundraise.com.au/page/Sandy_AlishaMHFBrainCancerNurses" target="_blank">https://mhfkokodatrek.gofundraise.com.au/page/Sandy_AlishaMHFBrainCancerNurses</a></p> <p>Launch Mama - <a href="https://www.instagram.com/launchmama_/" target="_blank">https://www.instagram.com/launchmama_/</a></p> <p>Flexible Unpaid Parental Leave (100 Days)<a href="https://www.fairwork.gov.au/tools-and-resources/fact-sheets/minimum-workplace-entitlements/parental-leave-and-related-entitlements#rules-taking-unpaid-leave" target="_blank">https://www.fairwork.gov.au/tools-and-resources/fact-sheets/minimum-workplace-entitlements/parental-leave-and-related-entitlements#rules-taking-unpaid-leave </a></p> <p>HOSTS &amp; PRODUCERS</p> <p>Kelly McCarren<strong> </strong><a href="http://www.instagram.com/kelly_mccarren/" target="_blank">⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠www.instagram.com/kelly_mccarren/⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠</a> </p> <p>Kee Reece <a href="http://www.instagram.com/keereece/" target="_blank">⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠www.instagram.com/keereece/⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠</a>  </p> <p>AUDIO PRODUCTION</p> <p>Claudia Coy <a href="https://podcasters.spotify.com/pod/dashboard/episode/www.hobohutmedia.com" target="_blank">⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠⁠https://www.instagram.com/claudia_coy/⁠</a></p> <p><br></p><p>See <a href="https://omnystudio.com/listener">omnystudio.com/listener</a> for privacy information.</p>]]></description>

      <title>The Truth About Daycare</title>
      <itunes:title>The Truth About Daycare</itunes:title>
      <description><![CDATA[<p>In this episode, we attempt to tackle the bug factory AKA daycare. This episode is perfect for parents who are considering sending their child to daycare OR just an unhinged lol with us (us also including HFM/RSV/GASTRO etc).</p> <p>We talk about our own experiences finding the right daycare and how we navigated the adjustment of being by their side all day to jumping back into our careers and all the fun little things no one tells you about daycare. </p> <p>Then later in the episode, we talk to Sh*tter Sally, who is not only a mother herself but runs the daycare that her son goes to! Sally unpacks the whole daycare experience - what you should be looking for when it comes to the right centre, how to make the transition easier &amp; all the things the educators wish you&#39;d remember. </p> <p>MENTIONS</p> <p>Holly Wainwright Article <a href="https://www.mamanatural.com/baby-updates/">https://www.mamamia.com.au/jobs-working-mothers-do-before-9am/</a></p> <p>HOSTS &amp; PRODUCERS</p> <p>Kelly McCarren<strong> </strong><a href="http://www.instagram.com/kelly_mccarren/">⁠⁠www.instagram.com/kelly_mccarren/⁠⁠</a> </p> <p>Kee Reece <a href="http://www.instagram.com/keereece/">⁠⁠www.instagram.com/keereece/⁠⁠</a>  </p> <p>AUDIO PRODUCTION</p> <p>Claudia Coy <a href="https://podcasters.spotify.com/pod/dashboard/episode/www.hobohutmedia.com">⁠⁠https://www.instagram.com/claudia_coy/</a></p><p>See <a href="https://omnystudio.com/listener">omnystudio.com/listener</a> for privacy information.</p>]]></description>
      <content:encoded><![CDATA[<p>In this episode, we attempt to tackle the bug factory AKA daycare. This episode is perfect for parents who are considering sending their child to daycare OR just an unhinged lol with us (us also including HFM/RSV/GASTRO etc).</p> <p>We talk about our own experiences finding the right daycare and how we navigated the adjustment of being by their side all day to jumping back into our careers and all the fun little things no one tells you about daycare. </p> <p>Then later in the episode, we talk to Sh*tter Sally, who is not only a mother herself but runs the daycare that her son goes to!       <title>Fkn Milestones</title>
      <itunes:title>Fkn Milestones</itunes:title>
      <description><![CDATA[<p>Milestones can cause pure panic for parents, especially first-timers. Designed as a guide to track whether a child&#39;s development is on track, the truth of it is they leave us feeling smug if the kid is miles ahead and like we’re failing if they’re nowhere near.</p> <p>In this ep, we breakdown the milestones that freaked us out the most &amp; how we dealt with the pressure of &#39;the timeline&#39;.</p> <p>Then later in the ep, we have a lovely Sh*tter, Beth joining us for a chat. Beth is a mother of 3 young boys (with another on the way!) who have each developed in very different ways, and on very different timelines.       <title>Will I Ever Sleep Again? How To Get Your Baby To Sleep</title>

      <title>"I Ended Up In A Psych Ward" - Postpartum Mental Health</title>
      <itunes:title>"I Ended Up In A Psych Ward" - Postpartum Mental Health</itunes:title>
      <description><![CDATA[<p><strong>Content Warning: </strong>This episode discusses themes that may be upsetting. We discuss postpartum depression and psychosis, suicidal ideation, overdose, severe mental health issues and disassociation. Listener discretion is advised. </p> <p><br></p> <p>The postpartum period can be one of the most isolating and lonely times of someone&#39;s life. You&#39;ve just grown and birthed an entire human, your hormones are all over the shop, and you&#39;re keeping your little one alive while sleep deprived and trying to remember the person you once were. It&#39;s often not a great recipe, yet we&#39;re still sold the idea of bliss being wrapped up in a &#39;newborn bubble&#39;. </p> <p><br></p> <p>In this episode of eat, sleep, sh*t, repeat, Kel and Kee discuss their own experiences with postpartum mental health and chat with someone whose experience led her to a psychiatric facility only weeks post-birth. This is an honest and raw conversation; let it remind you that you&#39;re never alone. </p> <p><br></p> <p>If you or someone you know is in crisis and needs help now, call triple zero (000). You can also call Lifeline on 13 11 14 — 24 hours a day, 7 days a week.</p> <p>PANDA (Perinatal Anxiety &amp; Depression Australia) supports women, men and families across Australia affected by anxiety and depression during pregnancy and in the first year of parenthood. Call 1300 726 306, 9am – 7:30pm AEST (Mon-Fri).</p> <p>Please visit <a href="https://www.healthdirect.gov.au/mental-health-helplines">https://www.healthdirect.gov.au/mental-health-helplines</a> to access additional free services. </p> <p><br></p> <p>CREDITS</p> <p>Hosts &amp; Producers: </p> <p>Kelly McCarren <a href="http://www.instagram.com/kelly_mccarren/">www.instagram.com/kelly_mccarren/</a> </p> <p>Kee Reece <a href="http://www.instagram.com/keereece/">www.instagram.com/keereece/</a>  </p> <p><br></p> <p>Audio Production: </p> <p>Pariya Taherzadeh <a href="http://www.instagram.com/pariya_peach_p/">www.instagram.com/pariya_peach_p/</a>  </p> <p><br></p> <p>Guest: </p> <p>Special thanks to <a href="mailto:megan@onebutmanypuzzles.com">Megan from One But Many Puzzles</a> for sharing her story <a href="https://www.onebutmanypuzzles.com.au/">www.onebutmanypuzzles.com.au/</a> </p> <p><br></p> <p>Thanks for listening!</p> <p><br></p><p>See <a href="https://omnystudio.com/listener">omnystudio.com/listener</a> for privacy information.</p>]]></description>

      <description><![CDATA[<p>Newsflash, babies need to be fed. And the only thing you feed them for the first 4-6 months of their lives is milk. But it’s not as straightforward as society might have you believe. </p> <p>If you’re under the opinion that #breastisbest, you can leave now, because this podcast isn’t for you.       <title>Postpartum Sex: What You Really Want To Know</title>
      <itunes:title>Postpartum Sex: What You Really Want To Know</itunes:title>
      <description><![CDATA[<p>Were you once a sexually ravenous beast but postpartum, the idea of intimacy makes you want to go through labour again? Or did your body change so much you feel disconnected from it? Maybe you’re hornier than ever but things aren’t working the way they used to?</p> <p><br></p> <p>In today’s episode, Kel and Kee discuss sex with a vulnerable and open manner you won’t hear anywhere else.
